A sudden release of water from the pool will spray directly onto passengers, easily causing injuries. No staff present.

Environment: The external environment is the ceiling of the hotels around Qingcheng Mountain. It is surrounded by mountains and rivers. The creek next to the hotel reminds me of the Kamogawa River in Kyoto.

Service: The front desk service is very good and professional, standard for a 5-star hotel, and the breakfast is particularly rich.

Overall, this hotel is a very cost-effective group purchase, with the same price as the Qingchengshan B&B I stayed at.
